     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestContext;
     4	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestFilter;
     5	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.PreMatching;
     6	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.UriBuilder;
     7	import jakarta.ws.rs.ext.Provider;
     8	import java.net.URI;
     9	
    10	@Provider
    11	@PreMatching
    12	public class S3VirtualHostFilter implements ContainerRequestFilter {
    13	
    14	    @Override
    15	    public void filter(ContainerRequestContext requestContext) {
    16	        String host = requestContext.getHeaderString("Host");
    17	        if (host == null) return;
    18	
    19	        // Pattern: bucket.localhost:4566 or bucket.s3.amazonaws.com or bucket.s3.region.amazonaws.com
    20	        if (host.contains(".localhost") || host.contains(".s3.")) {
    21	            int dotIndex = host.indexOf('.');
    22	            String bucket = host.substring(0, dotIndex);
    23	            
    24	            // Check if it's not just "s3" or "localhost"
    25	            if (bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("s3") || bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("localhost")) {
    26	                return;
    27	            }
    28	
    29	            URI uri = requestContext.getUriInfo().getRequestUri();
    30	            String path = uri.getRawPath();
    31	            
    32	            // Rewrite path from /key to /bucket/key
    33	            String newPath = "/" + bucket + (path.startsWith("/") ? "" : "/") + path;
    34	            
    35	            URI newUri = UriBuilder.fromUri(uri)
    36	                    .replacePath(newPath)
    37	                    .build();
    38	            
    39	            requestContext.setRequestUri(newUri);
    40	        }
    41	    }
    42	}
    43

    40	/**
    41	 * S3 controller handling REST-style S3 API requests.
    42	 * Routes: /{bucket} for bucket ops, /{bucket}/{key+} for object ops.
    43	 */
    44	@Path("/")
    45	public class S3Controller {
    46	
    47	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(S3Controller.class);
    48	    private static final DateTimeFormatter ISO_FORMAT = DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT;
    49	    private static final DateTimeFormatter RFC_822 = DateTimeFormatter
    50	            .ofPattern("EEE, dd MMM yyyy HH:mm:ss z", Locale.US)
    51	            .withZone(ZoneId.of("GMT"));
    52	
    53	    private final S3Service s3Service;
    54	    private final S3SelectService s3SelectService;
    55	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    56	
    57	    @Inject
    58	    public S3Controller(S3Service s3Service, S3SelectService s3SelectService,
    59	                        RegionResolver regionResolver) {
    60	        this.s3Service = s3Service;
    61	        this.s3SelectService = s3SelectService;
    62	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    // --- Bucket operations ---
    66	
    67	    @GET
    68	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
    69	    public Response listBuckets(@HeaderParam("X-Amz-Target") String target) {
    70	        if (target != null) {
    71	            return null;
    72	        }
    73	        try {
    74	            List<Bucket> buckets = s3Service.listBuckets();
    75	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
    76	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
    77	                    .start("ListAllMyBucketsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
    78	                    .start("Owner")
    79	                    .elem("ID", "owner")
    80	                    .elem("DisplayName", "owner")
    81	                    .end("Owner")
    82	                    .start("Buckets");
    83	            for (Bucket b : buckets) {
    84	                xml.start("Bucket")
    85	                   .elem("Name", b.getName())
    86	                   .elem("CreationDate", ISO_FORMAT.format(b.getCreationDate()))
    87	                   .end("Bucket");
    88	            }
    89	            xml.end("Buckets").end("ListAllMyBucketsResult");
    90	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
    91	        } catch (AwsException e) {
    92	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    @HEAD
    97	    @Path("/{bucket}")
    98	    public Response headBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket) {
    99	        try {
   100	            s3Service.headBucket(bucket);
   101	            String bucketRegion = s3Service.getBucketRegion(bucket);
   102	            if (bucketRegion == null || bucketRegion.isBlank()) {
   103	                bucketRegion = regionResolver.getDefaultRegion();
   104	            }
   105	            return Response.ok()
   106	                    .header("x-amz-bucket-region", bucketRegion)
   107	                    .build();
   108	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   109	            return Response.status(e.getHttpStatus()).build();
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	
   113	    @PUT

   115	    public Response createBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   116	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   117	                                  @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   118	                                  byte[] body) {
   119	        try {
   120	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "notification")) {

   122	            }
   123	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versioning")) {
   124	                return handlePutBucketVersioning(bucket, body);
   125	            }

   127	                return handlePutBucketTagging(bucket, body);
   128	            }
   129	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "object-lock")) {
   130	                return handlePutObjectLockConfiguration(bucket, body);
   131	            }
   132	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   133	                s3Service.putBucketPolicy(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   134	                return Response.ok().build();
   135	            }
   136	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   137	                s3Service.putBucketCors(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   138	                return Response.ok().build();
   139	            }
   140	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   141	                s3Service.putBucketLifecycle(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   142	                return Response.ok().build();
   143	            }
   144	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   145	                s3Service.putBucketAcl(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   146	                return Response.ok().build();
   147	            }
   148	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   149	                s3Service.putBucketEncryption(bucket, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   150	                return Response.ok().build();
   151	            }
   152	
   153	            String locationConstraint = null;
   154	            if (body != null && body.length > 0) {
   155	                locationConstraint = XmlParser.extractFirst(new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8),
   156	                        "LocationConstraint", null);
   157	            }
   158	            if (locationConstraint != null) {
   159	                locationConstraint = locationConstraint.trim();
   160	                if (locationConstraint.isEmpty()) {
   161	                    locationConstraint = null;
   162	                } else if ("us-east-1".equalsIgnoreCase(locationConstraint)) {
   163	                    throw new AwsException("InvalidLocationConstraint",
   164	                            "The specified location-constraint is not valid.", 400);
   165	                }
   166	            }
   167	            String region = locationConstraint != null ? locationConstraint : regionResolver.resolveRegion(httpHeaders);
   168	            s3Service.createBucket(bucket, region);
   169	            String lockEnabled = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-bucket-object-lock-enabled");
   170	            if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(lockEnabled)) {
   171	                s3Service.putBucketVersioning(bucket, "Enabled");
   172	                s3Service.setBucketObjectLockEnabled(bucket);
   173	            }
   174	            return Response.ok()
   175	                    .header("Location", "/" + bucket)
   176	                    .build();
   177	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   178	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   179	        }
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    @DELETE
   183	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   184	    public Response deleteBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   185	                                  @Context UriInfo uriInfo) {
   186	        try {
   187	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   188	                s3Service.deleteBucketTagging(bucket);
   189	                return Response.noContent().build();
   190	            }
   191	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   192	                s3Service.deleteBucketPolicy(bucket);
   193	                return Response.noContent().build();
   194	            }
   195	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   196	                s3Service.deleteBucketCors(bucket);
   197	                return Response.noContent().build();
   198	            }
   199	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   200	                s3Service.deleteBucketLifecycle(bucket);
   201	                return Response.noContent().build();
   202	            }
   203	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   204	                s3Service.deleteBucketEncryption(bucket);
   205	                return Response.noContent().build();
   206	            }
   207	            s3Service.deleteBucket(bucket);
   208	            return Response.noContent().build();
   209	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   210	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   211	        }
   212	    }

   214	    @GET
   215	    @Path("/{bucket}")
   216	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   217	    public Response listObjects(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   218	                                @QueryParam("prefix") String prefix,
   219	                                @QueryParam("delimiter") String delimiter,
   220	                                @QueryParam("max-keys") Integer maxKeys,
   221	                                @QueryParam("list-type") String listType,
   222	                                @QueryParam("continuation-token") String continuationToken,
   223	                                @QueryParam("start-after") String startAfter,
   224	                                @Context UriInfo uriInfo) {
   225	        try {
   226	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "uploads")) {
   227	                return handleListMultipartUploads(bucket);
   228	            }
   229	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "notification")) {
   230	                return handleGetBucketNotification(bucket);
   231	            }
   232	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versioning")) {
   233	                return handleGetBucketVersioning(bucket);
   234	            }
   235	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "versions")) {
   236	                return handleListObjectVersions(bucket, prefix, maxKeys);
   237	            }
   238	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "location")) {
   239	                return handleGetBucketLocation(bucket);
   240	            }
   241	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   242	                return handleGetBucketTagging(bucket);
   243	            }
   244	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "object-lock")) {
   245	                return handleGetObjectLockConfiguration(bucket);
   246	            }
   247	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "policy")) {
   248	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketPolicy(bucket)).build();
   249	            }
   250	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "cors")) {
   251	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketCors(bucket)).build();
   252	            }
   253	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "lifecycle")) {
   254	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketLifecycle(bucket)).build();
   255	            }
   256	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   257	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketAcl(bucket)).build();
   258	            }
   259	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "encryption")) {
   260	                return Response.ok(s3Service.getBucketEncryption(bucket)).build();
   261	            }
   262	
   263	            int max = (maxKeys != null && maxKeys > 0) ? maxKeys : 1000;
   264	            List<S3Object> objects = s3Service.listObjects(bucket, prefix, delimiter, max);
   265	            boolean v2 = "2".equals(listType);
   266	
   267	            XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   268	                    .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   269	                    .start("ListBucketResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   270	                    .elem("Name", bucket)
   271	                    .elem("Prefix", prefix)
   272	                    .elem("Delimiter", delimiter)
   273	                    .elem("MaxKeys", max);
   274	            if (v2) {
   275	                xml.elem("KeyCount", objects.size());
   276	            }
   277	            xml.elem("IsTruncated", false);
   278	            for (S3Object obj : objects) {
   279	                xml.start("Contents")
   280	                   .elem("Key", obj.getKey())
   281	                   .elem("LastModified", ISO_FORMAT.format(obj.getLastModified()))
   282	                   .elem("ETag", obj.getETag())
   283	                   .elem("Size", obj.getSize())
   284	                   .elem("StorageClass", obj.getStorageClass())
   285	                   .end("Contents");
   286	            }
   287	            xml.end("ListBucketResult");
   288	            return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
   289	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   290	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   291	        }
   292	    }

   294	    // --- Object operations ---
   295	
   296	    @PUT
   297	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   298	    public Response putObject(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   299	                              @PathParam("key") String key,
   300	                              @HeaderParam("Content-Type") String contentType,
   301	                              @HeaderParam("Content-Encoding") String contentEncoding,
   302	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-content-sha256") String contentSha256,
   303	                              @HeaderParam("x-amz-copy-source") String copySource,
   304	                              @QueryParam("uploadId") String uploadId,
   305	                              @QueryParam("partNumber") Integer partNumber,
   306	                              @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   307	                              @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   308	                              byte[] body) {
   309	        try {
   310	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "tagging")) {
   311	                return handlePutObjectTagging(bucket, key, body);
   312	            }
   313	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "retention")) {
   314	                return handlePutObjectRetention(bucket, key,
   315	                        uriInfo.getQueryParameters().getFirst("versionId"), httpHeaders, body);
   316	            }
   317	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "legal-hold")) {
   318	                return handlePutObjectLegalHold(bucket, key,
   319	                        uriInfo.getQueryParameters().getFirst("versionId"), body);
   320	            }
   321	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "acl")) {
   322	                s3Service.putObjectAcl(bucket, key, uriInfo.getQueryParameters().getFirst("versionId"),
   323	                        new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   324	                return Response.ok().build();
   325	            }
   326	
   327	            if (uploadId != null && partNumber != null) {
   328	                byte[] partData = decodeAwsChunked(body, contentEncoding, contentSha256);
   329	                validateChecksumHeaders(httpHeaders, partData);
   330	                String eTag = s3Service.uploadPart(bucket, key, uploadId, partNumber, partData);
   331	                return Response.ok().header("ETag", eTag).build();
   332	            }
   333	
   334	            if (copySource != null && !copySource.isEmpty()) {
   335	                return handleCopyObject(copySource, bucket, key, contentType, httpHeaders);
   336	            }
   337	
   338	            String lockMode = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-object-lock-mode");
   339	            String retainUntilStr = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-object-lock-retain-until-date");
   340	            String legalHold = httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-object-lock-legal-hold");
   341	            Instant retainUntil = retainUntilStr != null ? Instant.parse(retainUntilStr) : null;
   342	
   343	            byte[] data = decodeAwsChunked(body, contentEncoding, contentSha256);
   344	            validateChecksumHeaders(httpHeaders, data);
   345	            S3Object obj = s3Service.putObject(bucket, key, data, contentType, extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders),
   346	                    httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"),
   347	                    lockMode, retainUntil, legalHold);
   348	            var resp = Response.ok().header("ETag", obj.getETag());
   349	            if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   350	                resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   351	            }
   352	            appendObjectHeaders(resp, obj);
   353	            return resp.build();
   354	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   355	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);

   305	            .delete("/" + bucket)
   306	        .then()
   307	            .statusCode(204);
   308	    }
   309	
   310	    @Test
   311	    @Order(19)
   312	    void createBucketRejectsUsEast1LocationConstraint() {
   313	        String createBucketConfiguration = """
   314	                <CreateBucketConfiguration xmlns="http://s3.amazonaws.com/doc/2006-03-01/">
   315	                    <LocationConstraint>us-east-1</LocationConstraint>
   316	                </CreateBucketConfiguration>
   317	                """;
   318	
   319	        given()
   320	            .contentType("application/xml")
   321	            .body(createBucketConfiguration)
   322	        .when()
   323	            .put("/invalid-location-bucket")
   324	        .then()
   325	            .statusCode(400)
   326	            .body(containsString("InvalidLocationConstraint"));
   327	    }

    93	    public Bucket createBucket(String bucketName, String region) {
    94	        var existing = bucketStore.get(bucketName);
    95	        if (existing.isPresent()) {
    96	            throw new AwsException("BucketAlreadyOwnedByYou",
    97	                    "Your previous request to create the named bucket succeeded and you already own it.", 409);
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        Bucket bucket = new Bucket(bucketName);
   101	        bucket.setRegion(region);
   102	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   103	        LOG.infov("Created bucket: {0} in region: {1}", bucketName, region);
   104	        return bucket;
   105	    }
   106	
   107	    public void deleteBucket(String bucketName) {
   108	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   109	
   110	        // Check if bucket is empty
   111	        List<S3Object> objects = listObjects(bucketName, null, null, 1);
   112	        if (!objects.isEmpty()) {
   113	            throw new AwsException("BucketNotEmpty",
   114	                    "The bucket you tried to delete is not empty.", 409);
   115	        }
   116	
   117	        bucketStore.delete(bucketName);
   118	        deleteDirectory(dataRoot.resolve(bucketName));
   119	        LOG.infov("Deleted bucket: {0}", bucketName);
   120	    }

   138	    public S3Object putObject(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data,
   139	                              String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass,
   140	                              String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   141	        S3Object object = storeObject(bucketName, key, data, contentType, metadata, storageClass, null, null,
   142	                objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   143	        fireNotifications(bucketName, key, "ObjectCreated:Put", object);
   144	        return object;

   151	                                 String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata) {
   152	        return storeObject(bucketName, key, data, contentType, metadata, null, null, null,
   153	                null, null, null);
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    private S3Object storeObject(String bucketName, String key, byte[] data,
   157	                                 String contentType, Map<String, String> metadata, String storageClass,
   158	                                 S3Checksum checksum, List<Part> parts,
   159	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   160	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   161	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   162	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   163	
   164	        S3Object object = new S3Object(bucketName, key, data, contentType);
   165	        if (metadata != null) {
   166	            object.getMetadata().putAll(metadata);
   167	        }
   168	        object.setStorageClass(ObjectAttributeName.normalizeStorageClass(storageClass));
   169	        object.setChecksum(checksum != null ? copyChecksum(checksum) : buildChecksum(data, parts, false));
   170	        object.setParts(copyParts(parts));
   171	
   172	        if (bucket.isVersioningEnabled()) {
   173	            String versionId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   174	            object.setVersionId(versionId);
   175	            object.setLatest(true);
   176	
   177	            // Check lock protection on the current latest before overwriting
   178	            String latestKey = objectKey(bucketName, key);
   179	            objectStore.get(latestKey).ifPresent(prev -> {
   180	                if (prev.isLatest() && !prev.isDeleteMarker() && bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   181	                    checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   182	                }
   183	                if (prev.getVersionId() != null) {
   184	                    prev.setLatest(false);
   185	                    objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, prev.getVersionId()), prev);
   186	                }
   187	            });
   188	
   189	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   190	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   191	
   192	            // Store versioned copy and update latest pointer
   193	            objectStore.put(versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId), object);
   194	            objectStore.put(latestKey, object);
   195	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   196	            writeVersionedFile(bucketName, key, versionId, data);
   197	            LOG.debugv("Put versioned object: {0}/{1} v={2} ({3} bytes)", bucketName, key, versionId, data.length);
   198	        } else {
   199	            // Check lock protection on the existing object before overwriting
   200	            if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled()) {
   201	                objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key)).ifPresent(prev -> {
   202	                    if (!prev.isDeleteMarker()) {
   203	                        checkLockProtection(prev, false);
   204	                    }
   205	                });
   206	            }
   207	
   208	            // Apply lock fields from request or bucket default
   209	            applyObjectLock(object, bucket, objectLockMode, retainUntilDate, legalHoldStatus);
   210	
   211	            objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), object);
   212	            writeFile(bucketName, key, data);
   213	            LOG.debugv("Put object: {0}/{1} ({2} bytes)", bucketName, key, data.length);
   214	        }
   215	        return object;
   216	    }
   217	
   218	    private void applyObjectLock(S3Object object, Bucket bucket,
   219	                                 String objectLockMode, Instant retainUntilDate, String legalHoldStatus) {
   220	        if (objectLockMode != null) {
   221	            object.setObjectLockMode(objectLockMode);
   222	            object.setRetainUntilDate(retainUntilDate);
   223	        } else if (bucket.isObjectLockEnabled() && bucket.getDefaultRetention() != null) {
   224	            ObjectLockRetention def = bucket.getDefaultRetention();
   225	            object.setObjectLockMode(def.mode());
   226	            long days = "Years".equals(def.unit()) ? (long) def.value() * 365 : def.value();
   227	            object.setRetainUntilDate(Instant.now().plusSeconds(days * 86400L));
   228	        }
   229	        if (legalHoldStatus != null) {
   230	            object.setLegalHoldStatus(legalHoldStatus);
   231	        }
   232	    }
   233	
   234	    private void checkLockProtection(S3Object obj, boolean bypassGovernance) {
   235	        if ("ON".equals(obj.getLegalHoldStatus())) {
   236	            throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object has an active legal hold", 403);
   237	        }
   238	        if (obj.getRetainUntilDate() != null && Instant.now().isBefore(obj.getRetainUntilDate())) {
   239	            if ("COMPLIANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode())) {
   240	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by COMPLIANCE retention", 403);
   241	            }
   242	            if ("GOVERNANCE".equals(obj.getObjectLockMode()) && !bypassGovernance) {
   243	                throw new AwsException("AccessDenied", "Object is protected by GOVERNANCE retention", 403);
   244	            }
   245	        }
   246	    }
   247	
   248	    public S3Object getObject(String bucketName, String key) {
   249	        return getObject(bucketName, key, null);

   252	    public S3Object getObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   253	        S3Object obj = getObjectMetadata(bucketName, key, versionId);
   254	
   255	        // Read from versioned file if available, otherwise from latest
   256	        if (versionId != null) {
   257	            obj.setData(readVersionedFile(bucketName, key, versionId));
   258	        } else {
   259	            obj.setData(readFile(bucketName, key));
   260	        }
   261	        return obj;
   262	    }

   272	    public S3Object getObjectMetadata(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   273	        S3Object copy = copyObject(getStoredObject(bucketName, key, versionId));
   274	        copy.setData(null);

   277	
   278	    public GetObjectAttributesResult getObjectAttributes(String bucketName, String key, String versionId,
   279	                                                         Set<ObjectAttributeName> attributes,
   280	                                                         Integer maxParts, Integer partNumberMarker) {
   281	        S3Object object = getObjectMetadata(bucketName, key, versionId);
   282	
   283	        GetObjectAttributesResult result = new GetObjectAttributesResult();
   284	        result.setLastModified(object.getLastModified());
   285	        result.setVersionId(object.getVersionId());
   286	
   287	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.E_TAG)) {
   288	            result.setETag(object.getETag());
   289	        }
   290	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.STORAGE_CLASS)) {
   291	            result.setStorageClass(object.getStorageClass());
   292	        }
   293	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_SIZE)) {
   294	            result.setObjectSize(object.getSize());
   295	        }
   296	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.CHECKSUM)) {
   297	            result.setChecksum(copyChecksum(object.getChecksum()));
   298	        }
   299	        if (attributes.contains(ObjectAttributeName.OBJECT_PARTS)) {
   300	            result.setObjectParts(buildObjectParts(object, maxParts, partNumberMarker));
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        return result;
   304	    }
   305	
   306	    private S3Object getStoredObject(String bucketName, String key, String versionId) {
   307	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   308	
   309	        String storeKey = versionId != null ? versionedKey(bucketName, key, versionId) : objectKey(bucketName, key);
   310	        S3Object object = objectStore.get(storeKey)
   311	                .orElseThrow(() -> versionId != null
   312	                        ? new AwsException("NoSuchVersion", "The specified version does not exist.", 404)
   313	                        : new AwsException("NoSuchKey", "The specified key does not exist.", 404));
   314	        if (object.isDeleteMarker()) {
   315	            throw new AwsException("NoSuchKey", "The specified key does not exist.", 404);
   316	        }
   317	        return object;
   318	    }
   319	
   320	    private GetObjectAttributesParts buildObjectParts(S3Object object, Integer maxParts, Integer partNumberMarker) {
   321	        List<Part> sortedParts = new ArrayList<>(copyParts(object.getParts()));
   322	        sortedParts.sort(Comparator.comparingInt(Part::getPartNumber));
   323	
   324	        int max = (maxParts == null || maxParts <= 0) ? 1000 : maxParts;
   325	        int marker = Math.max(partNumberMarker != null ? partNumberMarker : 0, 0);
   326	
   327	        List<Part> visibleParts = sortedParts.stream()
   328	                .filter(part -> part.getPartNumber() > marker)
   329	                .toList();
   330	        List<Part> returnedParts = visibleParts.stream().limit(max).toList();
   331	
   332	        GetObjectAttributesParts result = new GetObjectAttributesParts();
   333	        result.setMaxParts(max);
   334	        result.setPartNumberMarker(marker);
   335	        result.setParts(returnedParts);
   336	        result.setPartsCount(sortedParts.size());
   337	        result.setTruncated(visibleParts.size() > returnedParts.size());
   338	        result.setNextPartNumberMarker(returnedParts.isEmpty()
   339	                ? marker
   340	                : returnedParts.get(returnedParts.size() - 1).getPartNumber());
   341	        return result;
   342	    }

   412	    public List<S3Object> listObjects(String bucketName, String prefix, String delimiter, int maxKeys) {
   413	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   414	
   415	        String keyPrefix = bucketName + "/";
   416	        String fullPrefix = prefix != null ? keyPrefix + prefix : keyPrefix;
   417	
   418	        // Filter out versioned entries (contain #v#) and delete markers
   419	        List<S3Object> allObjects = objectStore.scan(key ->
   420	                        key.startsWith(fullPrefix) && !key.contains("#v#"))
   421	                .stream()
   422	                .filter(obj -> !obj.isDeleteMarker())
   423	                .toList();
   424	        allObjects = new ArrayList<>(allObjects);
   425	
   426	        if (delimiter != null && !delimiter.isEmpty()) {
   427	            // Filter to only return objects at this level (simulate directory listing)
   428	            allObjects = allObjects.stream()
   429	                    .filter(obj -> {
   430	                        String remainder = obj.getKey().substring(prefix != null ? prefix.length() : 0);
   431	                        return !remainder.contains(delimiter);
   432	                    })
   433	                    .toList();
   434	        }
   435	
   436	        if (maxKeys > 0 && allObjects.size() > maxKeys) {
   437	            allObjects = allObjects.subList(0, maxKeys);
   438	        }
   439	
   440	        return allObjects;
   441	    }

   448	
   449	    public S3Object copyObject(String sourceBucket, String sourceKey,
   450	                               String destBucket, String destKey,
   451	                               String metadataDirective, Map<String, String> replacementMetadata,
   452	                               String storageClass, String contentType) {
   453	        S3Object source = getObject(sourceBucket, sourceKey);
   454	        ensureBucketExists(destBucket);
   455	
   456	        boolean replaceMetadata = "REPLACE".equalsIgnoreCase(metadataDirective);
   457	        Map<String, String> metadata = replaceMetadata ? new LinkedHashMap<>() : new LinkedHashMap<>(source.getMetadata());
   458	        if (replaceMetadata && replacementMetadata != null) {
   459	            metadata.putAll(replacementMetadata);
   460	        }
   461	
   462	        String effectiveContentType = replaceMetadata && contentType != null ? contentType : source.getContentType();
   463	        String effectiveStorageClass = storageClass != null ? storageClass : source.getStorageClass();
   464	        S3Object copy = storeObject(destBucket, destKey, source.getData(), effectiveContentType, metadata,
   465	                effectiveStorageClass, source.getChecksum(), source.getParts(), null, null, null);
   466	        copy.setETag(source.getETag());
   467	        LOG.debugv("Copied object: {0}/{1} -> {2}/{3}", sourceBucket, sourceKey, destBucket, destKey);
   468	        fireNotifications(destBucket, destKey, "ObjectCreated:Copy", copy);
   469	        return copy;
   470	    }

   539	    public DeleteObjectsResult deleteObjects(String bucketName, List<String> keys) {
   540	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   541	        List<DeleteResult> deleted = new ArrayList<>();
   542	        List<DeleteError> errors = new ArrayList<>();
   543	        for (String key : keys) {
   544	            try {
   545	                S3Object result = deleteObject(bucketName, key);
   546	                if (result != null && result.isDeleteMarker()) {

   553	            }
   554	        }
   555	        return new DeleteObjectsResult(deleted, errors);

   578	    public void deleteObjectTagging(String bucketName, String key) {
   579	        ensureBucketExists(bucketName);
   580	        S3Object obj = objectStore.get(objectKey(bucketName, key))
   581	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchKey",
   582	                        "The specified key does not exist.", 404));
   583	        obj.setTags(new java.util.HashMap<>());
   584	        objectStore.put(objectKey(bucketName, key), obj);
   585	        LOG.debugv("Deleted tags from object: {0}/{1}", bucketName, key);
   586	    }
   587	
   588	    // --- Bucket Tagging ---
   589	
   590	    public void putBucketTagging(String bucketName, Map<String, String> tags) {
   591	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   592	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   593	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   594	        bucket.setTags(tags != null ? tags : new java.util.HashMap<>());
   595	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   596	        LOG.debugv("Put tags on bucket: {0}", bucketName);
   597	    }
   598	
   599	    public Map<String, String> getBucketTagging(String bucketName) {
   600	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   601	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   602	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   603	        return bucket.getTags() != null ? bucket.getTags() : Map.of();
   604	    }
   605	
   606	    public void deleteBucketTagging(String bucketName) {
   607	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   608	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   609	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   610	        bucket.setTags(new java.util.HashMap<>());
   611	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   612	        LOG.debugv("Deleted tags from bucket: {0}", bucketName);
   613	    }
   614	
   615	    // --- Object Lock Configuration ---
   616	
   617	    public void setBucketObjectLockEnabled(String bucketName) {
   618	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   619	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   620	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   621	        bucket.setBucketObjectLockEnabled();
   622	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   623	        LOG.infov("Enabled Object Lock for bucket: {0}", bucketName);
   624	    }
   625	
   626	    public void putObjectLockConfiguration(String bucketName, String mode, String unit, int value) {
   627	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   628	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   629	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   630	        bucket.setBucketObjectLockEnabled();
   631	        if (mode != null && unit != null && value > 0) {
   632	            bucket.setDefaultRetention(new ObjectLockRetention(mode, unit, value));
   633	        } else {
   634	            bucket.setDefaultRetention(null);
   635	        }
   636	        bucketStore.put(bucketName, bucket);
   637	        LOG.infov("Set Object Lock configuration for bucket: {0}, mode={1}, unit={2}, value={3}",
   638	                bucketName, mode, unit, value);
   639	    }
   640	
   641	    public ObjectLockRetention getObjectLockConfiguration(String bucketName) {
   642	        Bucket bucket = bucketStore.get(bucketName)
   643	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("NoSuchBucket",
   644	                        "The specified bucket does not exist.", 404));
   645	        return bucket.getDefaultRetention();
   646	    }

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3;
     2	
     3	import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.XmlBuilder;
     4	import jakarta.inject.Inject;
     5	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestContext;
     6	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestFilter;
     7	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.MediaType;
     8	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.Response;
     9	import jakarta.ws.rs.ext.Provider;
    10	
    11	@Provider
    12	public class PreSignedUrlFilter implements ContainerRequestFilter {
    13	
    14	    private final PreSignedUrlGenerator presignGenerator;
    15	
    16	    @Inject
    17	    public PreSignedUrlFilter(PreSignedUrlGenerator presignGenerator) {
    18	        this.presignGenerator = presignGenerator;
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    @Override
    22	    public void filter(ContainerRequestContext requestContext) {
    23	        var queryParams = requestContext.getUriInfo().getQueryParameters();
    24	
    25	        // Only process if this is a pre-signed URL request
    26	        String algorithm = queryParams.getFirst("X-Amz-Algorithm");
    27	        if (algorithm == null) {
    28	            return;
    29	        }
    30	
    31	        String amzDate = queryParams.getFirst("X-Amz-Date");
    32	        String expiresStr = queryParams.getFirst("X-Amz-Expires");
    33	        String signature = queryParams.getFirst("X-Amz-Signature");
    34	
    35	        if (amzDate == null || expiresStr == null || signature == null) {
    36	            requestContext.abortWith(errorResponse(403, "AccessDenied",
    37	                    "Missing required pre-signed URL parameters."));
    38	            return;
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        int expires;
    42	        try {
    43	            expires = Integer.parseInt(expiresStr);
    44	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
    45	            requestContext.abortWith(errorResponse(403, "AccessDenied",
    46	                    "Invalid X-Amz-Expires value."));
    47	            return;
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        // Check expiration
    51	        if (presignGenerator.isExpired(amzDate, expires)) {
    52	            requestContext.abortWith(errorResponse(403, "AccessDenied",
    53	                    "Request has expired."));
    54	            return;
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        // Optionally verify signature (if validateSignatures is enabled)
    58	        if (presignGenerator.shouldValidateSignatures()) {
    59	            String path = requestContext.getUriInfo().getPath();
    60	            String[] parts = path.split("/", 3);
    61	            if (parts.length < 3) {
    62	                requestContext.abortWith(errorResponse(403, "AccessDenied",
    63	                        "Invalid pre-signed URL path."));
    64	                return;
    65	            }
    66	            String bucket = parts[1];
    67	            String key = parts[2];
    68	            String method = requestContext.getMethod();
    69	
    70	            if (!presignGenerator.verifySignature(method, bucket, key, amzDate, expires, signature)) {
    71	                requestContext.abortWith(errorResponse(403, "SignatureDoesNotMatch",
    72	                        "The request signature we calculated does not match the signature you provided."));
    73	            }
    74	        }
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    private Response errorResponse(int status, String code, String message) {
    78	        String xml = new XmlBuilder()
    79	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
    80	                .start("Error")
    81	                  .elem("Code", code)
    82	                  .elem("Message", message)
    83	                .end("Error")
    84	                .build();
    85	        return Response.status(status).entity(xml).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
    86	    }
    87	}

   473	    @POST
   474	    @Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")
   475	    @Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML)
   476	    public Response handleMultipartPost(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket,
   477	                                         @PathParam("key") String key,
   478	                                         @QueryParam("uploadId") String uploadId,
   479	                                         @QueryParam("versionId") String versionId,
   480	                                         @HeaderParam("Content-Type") String contentType,
   481	                                         @Context HttpHeaders httpHeaders,
   482	                                         @Context UriInfo uriInfo,
   483	                                         byte[] body) {
   484	        try {
   485	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "uploads")) {
   486	                MultipartUpload upload = s3Service.initiateMultipartUpload(bucket, key, contentType,
   487	                        extractUserMetadata(httpHeaders), httpHeaders.getHeaderString("x-amz-storage-class"));
   488	                String xml = new XmlBuilder()
   489	                        .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   490	                        .start("InitiateMultipartUploadResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   491	                        .elem("Bucket", bucket)
   492	                        .elem("Key", key)
   493	                        .elem("UploadId", upload.getUploadId())
   494	                        .end("InitiateMultipartUploadResult")
   495	                        .build();
   496	                return Response.ok(xml).build();
   497	            }
   498	
   499	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "restore")) {
   500	                s3Service.restoreObject(bucket, key, versionId, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   501	                return Response.accepted().build();
   502	            }
   503	
   504	            if (hasQueryParam(uriInfo, "select")) {
   505	                S3Object obj = s3Service.getObject(bucket, key, versionId);
   506	                byte[] result = s3SelectService.select(obj, new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
   507	                return Response.ok(result)
   508	                        .type("application/octet-stream")
   509	                        .build();
   510	            }
   511	
   512	            if (uploadId != null) {
   513	                List<Integer> partNumbers = parseCompleteMultipartBody(new String(body));
   514	                S3Object obj = s3Service.completeMultipartUpload(bucket, key, uploadId, partNumbers);
   515	                String baseUrl = uriInfo.getBaseUri().toString();
   516	                if (baseUrl.endsWith("/")) {
   517	                    baseUrl = baseUrl.substring(0, baseUrl.length() - 1);
   518	                }
   519	                XmlBuilder xmlBuilder = new XmlBuilder()
   520	                        .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   521	                        .start("CompleteMultipartUploadResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   522	                        .elem("Location", baseUrl + "/" + bucket + "/" + key)
   523	                        .elem("Bucket", bucket)
   524	                        .elem("Key", key)
   525	                        .elem("ETag", obj.getETag());
   526	                if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   527	                    xmlBuilder.elem("VersionId", obj.getVersionId());
   528	                }
   529	                String xml = xmlBuilder.end("CompleteMultipartUploadResult").build();
   530	                var resp = Response.ok(xml);
   531	                if (obj.getVersionId() != null) {
   532	                    resp.header("x-amz-version-id", obj.getVersionId());
   533	                }
   534	                return resp.build();
   535	            }
   536	
   537	            return xmlErrorResponse(new AwsException("InvalidArgument",
   538	                    "POST requires either ?uploads, ?uploadId, ?restore or ?select parameter.", 400));
   539	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   540	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   541	        }

   544	    private Response handleDeleteObjects(String bucket, byte[] body) {
   545	        String xml = new String(body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   546	        List<String> keys = XmlParser.extractAll(xml, "Key");
   547	        boolean quiet = XmlParser.containsValue(xml, "Quiet", "true");
   548	        S3Service.DeleteObjectsResult result = s3Service.deleteObjects(bucket, keys);
   549	
   550	        XmlBuilder builder = new XmlBuilder()
   551	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   552	                .start("DeleteResult", AwsNamespaces.S3);
   553	        if (!quiet) {
   554	            for (S3Service.DeleteResult d : result.deleted()) {
   555	                builder.start("Deleted").elem("Key", d.key());
   556	                if (d.deleteMarker()) {
   557	                    builder.elem("DeleteMarker", true);
   558	                    if (d.deleteMarkerVersionId() != null) {
   559	                        builder.elem("DeleteMarkerVersionId", d.deleteMarkerVersionId());
   560	                    }
   561	                }
   562	                builder.end("Deleted");
   563	            }
   564	        }
   565	        for (S3Service.DeleteError e : result.errors()) {
   566	            builder.start("Error")
   567	                   .elem("Key", e.key())
   568	                   .elem("Code", e.code())
   569	                   .elem("Message", e.message())
   570	                   .end("Error");
   571	        }
   572	        builder.end("DeleteResult");
   573	        return Response.ok(builder.build()).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
   574	    }

   576	    private Response handleListMultipartUploads(String bucket) {
   577	        List<MultipartUpload> uploads = s3Service.listMultipartUploads(bucket);
   578	        XmlBuilder xml = new XmlBuilder()
   579	                .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
   580	                .start("ListMultipartUploadsResult", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   581	                .elem("Bucket", bucket);
   582	        for (MultipartUpload upload : uploads) {
   583	            xml.start("Upload")
   584	               .elem("Key", upload.getKey())
   585	               .elem("UploadId", upload.getUploadId())
   586	               .elem("Initiated", ISO_FORMAT.format(upload.getInitiated()))
   587	               .end("Upload");
   588	        }
   589	        xml.end("ListMultipartUploadsResult");
   590	        return Response.ok(xml.build()).build();
   591	    }

   593	    private List<Integer> parseCompleteMultipartBody(String xml) {
   594	        List<String> parts = XmlParser.extractAll(xml, "PartNumber");
   595	        if (parts.isEmpty()) {
   596	            throw new AwsException("MalformedXML",
   597	                    "The XML you provided was not well-formed.", 400);
   598	        }
   599	        return parts.stream().map(Integer::parseInt).toList();
   600	    }

   693	    private Response handlePutBucketNotification(String bucket, byte[] body) {

   696	            NotificationConfiguration config = new NotificationConfiguration();
   697	
   698	            var queueConfigs = XmlParser.extractGroupsMulti(xml, "QueueConfiguration");
   699	            for (var group : queueConfigs) {
   700	                String id = group.getOrDefault("Id", List.of("")).get(0);
   701	                List<String> queueArns = group.get("Queue");
   702	                List<String> events = group.get("Event");

   706	            }
   707	
   708	            var topicConfigs = XmlParser.extractGroupsMulti(xml, "TopicConfiguration");

   710	                String id = group.getOrDefault("Id", List.of("")).get(0);
   711	                List<String> topicArns = group.get("Topic");
   712	                List<String> events = group.get("Event");
   713	                if (topicArns != null && !topicArns.isEmpty() && events != null && !events.isEmpty()) {
   714	                    config.getTopicConfigurations().add(new TopicNotification(id, topicArns.get(0), events));
   715	                }
   716	            }
   717	
   718	            s3Service.putBucketNotificationConfiguration(bucket, config);
   719	            return Response.ok().build();
   720	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   721	            return xmlErrorResponse(e);
   722	        }
   723	    }
   724	
   725	    // --- AWS Chunked Decoding ---
   726	
   727	    /**
   728	     * Decodes aws-chunked transfer encoding used by AWS SDK v2 with SigV4 chunk signing.
   729	     * Format: hex-size;chunk-signature=sig\r\n data \r\n ... 0;chunk-signature=sig\r\n
   730	     */
   731	    private byte[] decodeAwsChunked(byte[] body, String contentEncoding, String contentSha256) {
   732	        boolean isAwsChunked = (contentEncoding != null && contentEncoding.contains("aws-chunked"))
   733	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD".equals(contentSha256)
   734	                || "STREAMING-AWS4-HMAC-SHA256-PAYLOAD-TRAILER".equals(contentSha256);
   735	        if (!isAwsChunked) {
   736	            return body;
   737	        }
   738	
   739	        try {
   740	            ByteArrayOutputStream out = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
   741	            String raw = new String(body, StandardCharsets.ISO_8859_1);
   742	            int pos = 0;
   743	            while (pos < raw.length()) {
   744	                int lineEnd = raw.indexOf('\n', pos);
   745	                if (lineEnd < 0) break;
   746	                String line = raw.substring(pos, lineEnd).trim();
   747	                int semiColon = line.indexOf(';');
   748	                String hexSize = semiColon >= 0 ? line.substring(0, semiColon) : line;
   749	                int chunkSize = Integer.parseInt(hexSize.trim(), 16);
   750	                if (chunkSize == 0) break;
   751	
   752	                int dataStart = lineEnd + 1;
   753	                byte[] chunkData = new byte[chunkSize];
   754	                System.arraycopy(body, dataStart, chunkData, 0, chunkSize);
   755	                out.write(chunkData);
   756	
   757	                pos = dataStart + chunkSize;
   758	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\r') pos++;
   759	                if (pos < raw.length() && raw.charAt(pos) == '\n') pos++;
   760	            }
   761	            return out.toByteArray();
   762	        } catch (Exception e) {
   763	            LOG.debugv("Failed to decode aws-chunked body, using raw: {0}", e.getMessage());
   764	            return body;
   765	        }
   766	    }
   767

   777	                .start("LocationConstraint", AwsNamespaces.S3)
   778	                .raw(XmlBuilder.escape(region))
   779	                .end("LocationConstraint")
   780	                .build();

    48	    }

    52	    }
    53	
    54	    public String generatePresignedUrl(String baseUrl, String bucket, String key,
    55	                                         String method, int expiresSeconds) {
    56	        int expiry = expiresSeconds > 0 ? expiresSeconds : defaultExpiry;
    57	        String amzDate = AMZ_DATE_FORMAT.format(Instant.now());
    58	        String credential = "AKIAIOSFODNN7EXAMPLE/" + amzDate.substring(0, 8) + "/" + defaultRegion + "/s3/aws4_request";
    59	
    60	        String signature = computeSignature(method, bucket, key, amzDate, expiry);
    61	
    62	        return baseUrl + "/" + bucket + "/" + key
    63	                + "?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256"
    64	                + "&X-Amz-Credential=" + URLEncoder.encode(credential, StandardCharsets.UTF_8)
    65	                + "&X-Amz-Date=" + amzDate
    66	                + "&X-Amz-Expires=" + expiry
    67	                + "&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host"
    68	                + "&X-Amz-Signature=" + signature;
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    public boolean isExpired(String amzDate, int expiresSeconds) {
    72	        try {
    73	            Instant signedAt = Instant.from(AMZ_DATE_FORMAT.parse(amzDate));
    74	            return Instant.now().isAfter(signedAt.plusSeconds(expiresSeconds));
    75	        } catch (Exception e) {
    76	            return true;
    77	        }
    78	    }
    79

    81	                                     String amzDate, int expiresSeconds, String signature) {
    82	        String expected = computeSignature(method, bucket, key, amzDate, expiresSeconds);
    83	        return expected.equals(signature);
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    private String computeSignature(String method, String bucket, String key,
    87	                                      String amzDate, int expiresSeconds) {
    88	        String stringToSign = method + "\n" + bucket + "/" + key + "\n" + amzDate + "\n" + expiresSeconds;
    89	        return hmacSha256(secret, stringToSign);
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    private static String hmacSha256(String secret, String data) {
    93	        try {
    94	            Mac mac = Mac.getInstance("HmacSHA256");
    95	            mac.init(new SecretKeySpec(secret.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), "HmacSHA256"));
    96	            byte[] hash = mac.doFinal(data.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    97	            var sb = new StringBuilder();
    98	            for (byte b : hash) {
    99	                sb.append(String.format("%02x", b));
   100	            }
   101	            return sb.toString();
   102	        } catch (Exception e) {
   103	            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to compute HMAC-SHA256", e);
   104	        }
   105	    }
   106	}

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.s3;
     2	
     3	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestContext;
     4	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.ContainerRequestFilter;
     5	import jakarta.ws.rs.container.PreMatching;
     6	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.UriBuilder;
     7	import jakarta.ws.rs.ext.Provider;
     8	import java.net.URI;
     9	
    10	@Provider
    11	@PreMatching
    12	public class S3VirtualHostFilter implements ContainerRequestFilter {
    13	
    14	    @Override
    15	    public void filter(ContainerRequestContext requestContext) {
    16	        String host = requestContext.getHeaderString("Host");
    17	        if (host == null) return;
    18	
    19	        // Pattern: bucket.localhost:4566 or bucket.s3.amazonaws.com or bucket.s3.region.amazonaws.com
    20	        if (host.contains(".localhost") || host.contains(".s3.")) {
    21	            int dotIndex = host.indexOf('.');
    22	            String bucket = host.substring(0, dotIndex);
    23	            
    24	            // Check if it's not just "s3" or "localhost"
    25	            if (bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("s3") || bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("localhost")) {
    26	                return;
    27	            }
    28	
    29	            URI uri = requestContext.getUriInfo().getRequestUri();
    30	            String path = uri.getRawPath();
    31	            
    32	            // Rewrite path from /key to /bucket/key
    33	            String newPath = "/" + bucket + (path.startsWith("/") ? "" : "/") + path;
    34	            
    35	            URI newUri = UriBuilder.fromUri(uri)
    36	                    .replacePath(newPath)
    37	                    .build();
    38	            
    39	            requestContext.setRequestUri(newUri);
    40	        }
    41	    }
    42	}

   420	
   421	    private String fetchTemplateFromS3(String url) {
   422	        try {
   423	            // Parse S3 URL: http://host:port/bucket/key or https://bucket.s3.amazonaws.com/key
   424	            String bucket;
   425	            String key;
   426	            if (url.contains(".s3.amazonaws.com") || url.contains(".s3.")) {
   427	                // Virtual-hosted: https://bucket.s3.region.amazonaws.com/key
   428	                String host = url.replaceFirst("https?://", "").split("/")[0];
   429	                bucket = host.split("\\.")[0];
   430	                key = url.substring(url.indexOf('/', url.indexOf("://") + 3) + 1);
   431	            } else {
   432	                // Path-style: http://host:port/bucket/key
   433	                String path = url.replaceFirst("https?://[^/]+/", "");
   434	                int slash = path.indexOf('/');
   435	                bucket = slash > 0 ? path.substring(0, slash) : path;
   436	                key = slash > 0 ? path.substring(slash + 1) : "";
   437	            }
   438	            var obj = s3Service.getObject(bucket, key);
   439	            return new String(obj.getData());
   440	        } catch (Exception e) {
   441	            LOG.warnv("Failed to fetch template from {0}: {1}", url, e.getMessage());
   442	            return "{}";
   443	        }
   444	    }
   445

2026-05-30 04:01:31,582 - INFO - swea-agent-floci-io__floci-88 - 💭 THOUGHT
Interesting! These tests use `Host: bucket.localhost` header to simulate virtual-hosted-style access. The tests PUT to `/` to create a bucket and PUT to `/{key}` to create objects, etc.

But wait - when someone uses `Host: bucket.localhost` with path `/`, the S3VirtualHostFilter rewrites it to `/{bucket}/` which would match the `createBucket` handler (PUT `/{bucket}`). When someone uses `Host: bucket.localhost` with path `/key`, it rewrites to `/{bucket}/key` which matches the putObject handler.

But what about GET `/` with `Host: bucket.localhost`? That should list objects in the bucket. Let me trace through the filter logic...

With `Host: bucket.localhost` and path `/`:
- `host.contains(".localhost")` → true
- `dotIndex = host.indexOf('.')` → 6
- `bucket = host.substring(0, 6)` → "bucket"
- `newPath = "/" + "bucket" + "" + "/"` → "/bucket/"
- So URI becomes `/bucket/`

With `Host: bucket.localhost` and path `/key`:
- `newPath = "/" + "bucket" + "" + "/key"` → "/bucket/key"

That seems correct.

But wait, what about the `listBuckets` method at GET `/` without a bucket in the host? That should still work as before. The filter only rewrites when `host.contains(".localhost") || host.contains(".s3.")`.

Now let me think about what might be broken. Let me look at the PreSignedUrlFilter again, particularly at this part:

```java
String path = requestContext.getUriInfo().getPath();
String[] parts = path.split("/", 3);
if (parts.length < 3) {
    ...
}
String bucket = parts[1];
String key = parts[2];
```

The `parts[0]` would be empty string (since path starts with `/`). `parts[1]` would be the bucket, `parts[2]` would be the key. For path `/bucket/key`, this gives `["", "bucket", "key"]` → correct.

But what if the path is just `/` (for list buckets)? Then `parts` would be `["", ""]` with length 2. The filter would abort with "Invalid pre-signed URL path." But list buckets doesn't use pre-signed URLs typically.

OK, all tests pass. Let me look more broadly at what changes might be expected. Let me run the full test suite to see if any test fails:

Let me think about this differently. The PR description mentions "Support virtual paths in S3" and links to two AWS docs about path-style and virtual-hosted-style access. "Path style requests will be removed and are effectively deprecated" - this is a justification for why they need virtual-hosted-style support.

Looking at the S3VirtualHostFilter, it already converts virtual-hosted-style requests to path-style. But maybe there's an issue with how it handles certain edge cases:

1. What about when the host is `bucket.s3.region.amazonaws.com`? The filter checks `host.contains(".s3.")` which would match this.
2. What about `bucket.s3.amazonaws.com`? Same check works.
3. What about `bucket.localhost`? The filter checks `host.contains(".localhost")` which matches.

But wait - what about `bucket.localhost:4566`? The host header typically includes the port. So `host.contains(".localhost")` would be `"bucket.localhost:4566".contains(".localhost")` → true. Good.

Let me look at the S3VirtualHostFilter more carefully. I notice a potential bug:

```java
String newPath = "/" + bucket + (path.startsWith("/") ? "" : "/") + path;
```

If `path` is `/` (just root), then `newPath` = `"/" + bucket + "" + "/"` = `"/bucket/"`. This should match `@Path("/{bucket}")` endpoints.

If `path` is `/key` (just object key), then `newPath` = `"/" + bucket + "" + "/key"` = `"/bucket/key"`. This should match `@Path("/{bucket}/{key:.+}")` endpoints.

But what if path is already `/bucket/key` (someone sent a path-style request to a virtual host)? Then `newPath` = `"/" + bucket + "" + "/bucket/key"` = `"/bucket/bucket/key"` which would be wrong.

However, in practice, if someone uses virtual-hosted-style, they shouldn't be including the bucket in the path. So this shouldn't be an issue.

Now let me think about what could actually be missing. Let me look at the full list of files and see if there's something obvious I'm missing.

Let me check if there's an S3Controller that handles the root path properly for both styles:

Looking at the S3Controller:
- `@GET` on `/` → listBuckets
- `@HEAD` on `/{bucket}` → headBucket
- `@PUT` on `/{bucket}` → createBucket
- `@DELETE` on `/{bucket}` → deleteBucket
- `@GET` on `/{bucket}` → listObjects
- `@PUT` on `/{bucket}/{key:.+}` → putObject
- `@GET` on `/{bucket}/{key:.+}` → getObject
- `@HEAD` on `/{bucket}/{key:.+}` → headObject
- `@DELETE` on `/{bucket}/{key:.+}` → deleteObject
- `@POST` on `/{bucket}` → handleBucketPost
- `@POST` on `/{bucket}/{key:.+}` → handleMultipartPost

This all looks correct. The S3VirtualHostFilter handles converting virtual-hosted-style to path-style.

But wait - the `createBucket` method returns a `Location` header of `"/" + bucket`. When the client receives this, it would interpret it as path-style. That's probably fine.

Now let me check if there's something wrong with how the filter handles the root path when creating buckets. Let me trace through again:

1. Request: `PUT /` with `Host: mybucket.localhost`
2. S3VirtualHostFilter:

   - `host.contains(".localhost")` → true

"[FEAT] Support virtual paths in S3"

And links to:
- path-style-access
- virtual-hosted-style-access

"Path style requests will be removed and are effectively deprecated"

This seems to be saying that AWS is deprecating path-style access, so the emulator should support virtual-hosted-style access. The S3VirtualHostFilter already does this.

But maybe the issue is that the S3VirtualHostFilter doesn't properly handle all cases, or there's another component that needs to support virtual-hosted-style.

Let me look at the S3Controller more carefully. When it returns a `Location` header for `createBucket`, it returns `"/" + bucket`. When someone uses virtual-hosted-style, they might expect a different location.

But wait, all tests pass. Let me check if there might be a missing file or a test that's been added but is failing...

Actually, let me look at the S3SelectIntegrationTest more carefully. Those tests use `Host: bucket.localhost` header. But they PUT to `/` to create a bucket and PUT to `/{key}` to put objects.

When PUT to `/` with `Host: bucket.localhost`, the S3VirtualHostFilter rewrites to `PUT /bucket/`. The S3Controller's `createBucket` at `PUT /{bucket}` handles this. But the response includes `Location: /bucket`. Is this correct for virtual-hosted-style?

For virtual-hosted-style, the Location should probably be the path without the bucket (since the bucket is in the host). But the AWS S3 API actually returns the full URL in the Location header for virtual-hosted-style. So this might be fine.

    10	    @WithDefault("http://localhost:4566")
    11	    String baseUrl();
    12	
    13	    /**
    14	     * When set, overrides the hostname in base-url for URLs returned in API responses
    15	     * (e.g. SQS QueueUrl, SNS TopicArn). This is needed in multi-container Docker setups
    16	     * where "localhost" in the response URL would resolve to the wrong container.
    17	     *
    18	     * Example: FLOCI_HOSTNAME=floci makes SQS return
    19	     * http://floci:4566/000000000000/my-queue instead of http://localhost:4566/...
    20	     *
    21	     * Equivalent to LocalStack's LOCALSTACK_HOSTNAME.
    22	     */
    23	    Optional<String> hostname();
    24	
    25	    /**
    26	     * Returns the effective base URL, taking hostname into account.
    27	     * If hostname is set, replaces the host in baseUrl with it.
    28	     */
    29	    default String effectiveBaseUrl() {
    30	        return hostname()
    31	                .map(h -> baseUrl().replaceFirst("://[^:/]+(:\\d+)?", "://" + h + "$1"))

I noticed the `completeMultipartUpload` method builds a Location URL:\n\n```java\nString baseUrl = uriInfo.getBaseUri().toString();\nif (baseUrl.endsWith("/")) {\n    baseUrl = baseUrl.substring(0, baseUrl.length() - 1);\n}\nXmlBuilder xmlBuilder = new XmlBuilder()\n    ...\n    .elem("Location", baseUrl + "/" + bucket + "/" + key)\n```\n\nThis uses the path-style URL. But for virtual-hosted-style, the URL should be `http://bucket.s3.amazonaws.com/key`. However, this is a minor detail and AWS S3 actually returns path-style in the Location for compatibility.\n\nLet me now think about this problem differently. I\'ve been going around in circles. Let me look at the S3VirtualHostFilter one more time and think about what might need to change.\n\nThe filter:\n1. Gets the Host header\n2. If host matches `.localhost` or `.s3.`, extracts bucket name from the first segment\n3. Rewrites path from `/key` to `/bucket/key`\n\nBut what about when the host is something like `my-bucket.s3.localhost`? The filter would match `.s3.` and extract `my-bucket` as the bucket. But wait, `s3.localhost` is not a real AWS endpoint... Actually, in a local testing environment, you might use `bucket.s3.localhost` to simulate S3 virtual hosting. Let me check if the filter handles this:\n\n`"my-bucket.s3.localhost".contains(".s3.")` → true\n`"my-bucket.s3.localhost".contains(".localhost")` → true (both conditions match)\n\nHmm, let me think about the `.contains(".s3.")` check more carefully. What if someone sends Host: `mys3bucket.localhost`? \n\n`"mys3bucket.localhost".contains(".s3.")` → false (no `.s3.` substring)\n`"mys3bucket.localhost".contains(".localhost")` → true\n\nSo `bucket = "mys3bucket"`. That\'s correct.\n\nWhat about Host: `s3.localhost`?\n`"s3.localhost".contains(".s3.")` → false\n`"s3.localhost".contains(".localhost")` → true\n`bucket = "s3"` → but then it returns because bucket equals "s3". Correct!\n\nWhat about Host: `s3.amazonaws.com` (path-style)?\n`"s3.amazonaws.com".contains(".s3.")` → false (no dot before s3)\nSo it falls through correctly.\n\nOK, I think the filter logic is sound for common cases.\n\nLet me now try to think about what the PR might actually be requiring. Maybe I need to look at the PR from the perspective of the S3 controller - perhaps the controller currently ONLY supports path-style and the virtual host filter was recently added but doesn\'t cover all cases, or perhaps there\'s a missing piece in the S3Controller for handling virtual paths.\n\nWait, I just realized something. Let me look at the PreSignedUrlFilter again:\n\n```java\nString path = requestContext.getUriInfo().getPath();\nString[] parts = path.split("/", 3);\nif (parts.length < 3) {\n    requestContext.abortWith(errorResponse(403, "AccessDenied",\n            "Invalid pre-signed URL path."));\n    return;\n}\nString bucket = parts[1];\nString key = parts[2];\n```\n\nThis runs AFTER S3VirtualHostFilter (since it\'s not @PreMatching). So the path should already be rewritten. But what if someone sends a pre-signed URL that was generated for virtual-hosted-style?         return null;
```java
    }
    ...
}
```

This is on `@Path("/")` (the class-level path). So it only matches `GET /`. The `listObjects` is on `@Path("/{bucket}")`, so it matches `GET /bucketName`.

// Let me trace through the filter logic for various scenarios

public class VirtualHostTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        // Test various host headers
        String[] hosts = {
            "mybucket.localhost",
            "mybucket.localhost:4566", 
            "mybucket.s3.amazonaws.com",
            "mybucket.s3.us-east-1.amazonaws.com",
            "s3.amazonaws.com",
            "localhost",
            "localhost:4566",
            "mybucket.s3.localhost",
            "mybucket.s3.localhost:4566",
            "s3.localhost",
            "my.bucket.localhost",
            "my-bucket.s3.dualstack.us-east-1.amazonaws.com"
        };
        
        for (String host : hosts) {
            boolean matches = host.contains(".localhost") || host.contains(".s3.");
            if (matches) {
                int dotIndex = host.indexOf('.');
                String bucket = host.substring(0, dotIndex);
                boolean shouldSkip = bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("s3") || bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("localhost");
                System.out.println("Host: " + host + " -> matches=" + matches + ", bucket=" + bucket + ", skip=" + shouldSkip);
            } else {
                System.out.println("Host: " + host + " -> matches=" + matches + " (no rewrite)");
            }
        }
        
        // Test path rewriting
        String[][] tests = {
            {"/", "mybucket", "/mybucket/"},
            {"/key", "mybucket", "/mybucket/key"},
            {"/key/subkey", "mybucket", "/mybucket/key/subkey"},
            {"/key?foo=bar", "mybucket", "/mybucket/key?foo=bar"}, // rawPath doesn't include query
        };

        for (String[] test : tests) {
            String path = test[0];
            String bucket = test[1];

            System.out.println("path=" + path + " -> " + newPath + " (expected: " + expected + ") " + (newPath.equals(expected) ? "OK" : "FAIL"));
        }
    }
}

Wait, I just had another idea. Let me look at the PreSignedUrlGenerator more carefully. It generates URLs like:

```
baseUrl + "/" + bucket + "/" + key + "?X-Amz-Algorithm=..."
```

If `baseUrl` is `http://localhost:4566`, the URL is `http://localhost:4566/bucket/key?...`. This is path-style.

For virtual-hosted-style, the URL should be `http://bucket.localhost:4566/key?...`. But the generator doesn't support this.

However, the PreSignedUrlFilter validates these URLs. When a virtual-hosted request comes in with a pre-signed URL, the filter needs to verify the signature. Let me trace through:

1. Pre-signed URL generated for path-style: `http://localhost:4566/bucket/key?X-Amz-Algorithm=...`
2. Client sends request to virtual host: `http://bucket.localhost:4566/key?X-Amz-Algorithm=...`
3. S3VirtualHostFilter rewrites to: `/bucket/key?X-Amz-Algorithm=...`
4. PreSignedUrlFilter sees path `/bucket/key`, splits to bucket="bucket", key="key"
5. Verifies signature - but wait, the signature was computed for the path-style URL!

The signature computation in `PreSignedUrlGenerator.computeSignature`:
```java
String stringToSign = method + "\n" + bucket + "/" + key + "\n" + amzDate + "\n" + expiresSeconds;
```

This doesn't include the host or base URL, so it should be the same for both path-style and virtual-hosted-style. Good.

So the PreSignedUrlFilter should work with both styles.

Let me try yet another approach: maybe the issue is in the S3VirtualHostFilter itself and there's a bug that isn't caught by existing tests. Let me look at it one more time with fresh eyes:

```java
@Override
public void filter(ContainerRequestContext requestContext) {
    String host = requestContext.getHeaderString("Host");
    if (host == null) return;

    // Pattern: bucket.localhost:4566 or bucket.s3.amazonaws.com or bucket.s3.region.amazonaws.com
    if (host.contains(".localhost") || host.contains(".s3.")) {
        int dotIndex = host.indexOf('.');
        String bucket = host.substring(0, dotIndex);
        
        // Check if it's not just "s3" or "localhost"
        if (bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("s3") || bucket.equalsIgnoreCase("localhost")) {
            return;
        }

        URI uri = requestContext.getUriInfo().getRequestUri();
        String path = uri.getRawPath();
        
        // Rewrite path from /key to /bucket/key
        String newPath = "/" + bucket + (path.startsWith("/") ? "" : "/") + path;
        
        URI newUri = UriBuilder.fromUri(uri)
                .replacePath(newPath)
                .build();
        
        requestContext.setRequestUri(newUri);
    }
}
```

Wait, I see a potential issue! The `host.contains(".localhost")` check. What if the host is just `localhost` (no subdomain)? Then `host.contains(".localhost")` is false because there's no dot before `localhost`. But `host.contains(".s3.")` would also be false. So it correctly doesn't rewrite. Good.

But what if the host is `subdomain.localhost` (where subdomain is actually a bucket name)? The filter would extract `subdomain` as the bucket name and rewrite the path. This is correct for virtual-hosted-style.

Now, what about the `host.contains(".s3.")` check? What if someone uses `bucket.s3.localhost`? Both conditions match (`.s3.` and `.localhost`). The filter extracts `bucket` from the first dot. But wait, what if the host is `s3.localhost` (no bucket)? 
- `host.contains(".s3.")` → false (no `.s3.` substring)
- `host.contains(".localhost")` → true
- `dotIndex = 2`
- `bucket = "s3"` → skips because bucket equals "s3"

That's correct. What about `s3.amazonaws.com`?
- `host.contains(".s3.")` → false (no dot before s3)
- `host.contains(".localhost")` → false
- No rewrite. Correct!

But what about `bucket.amazonaws.com` (no s3)? 
- `host.contains(".s3.")` → false
- `host.contains(".localhost")` → false
- No rewrite. Correct (this isn't an S3 endpoint).

What about `bucket.s3.amazonaws.com`?
- `host.contains(".s3.")` → true
- `bucket = "bucket"`. Correct!

I think the filter is correct. Let me try to check if there's something missing in the S3Controller for handling virtual-hosted requests.

Actually, I just realized something. Let me look at the `createBucket` method in S3Controller more carefully:

```java
@PUT
@Path("/{bucket}")
public Response createBucket(@PathParam("bucket") String bucket, ...) {
    ...
    return Response.ok()
            .header("Location", "/" + bucket)
            .build();
}
```

When using virtual-hosted-style to create a bucket:
1. Request: `PUT /` with `Host: newbucket.localhost`
2. S3VirtualHostFilter rewrites to `PUT /newbucket/`
3. S3Controller matches `@PUT @Path("/{bucket}")` with bucket="newbucket"
4. Returns `Location: /newbucket`

The Location header `/newbucket` is path-style. For virtual-hosted-style, the client might expect just `/` (since the bucket is in the hostname). But AWS S3's actual response includes the full URL or path. I don't think this is the issue.

Let me look at the `handleGetBucketLocation` method:

```java
private Response handleGetBucketLocation(String bucket) {
    String region = s3Service.getBucketRegion(bucket);
    if (region == null) {
        region = regionResolver.getDefaultRegion();
    }
    String xml = new XmlBuilder()
            .raw("<?xml version=\"1.0\" encoding=\"UTF-8\"?>")
            .start("LocationConstraint", AwsNamespaces.S3)
            .raw(XmlBuilder.escape(region))
            .end("LocationConstraint")
            .build();
    return Response.ok(xml).type(MediaType.APPLICATION_XML).build();
}
```

This returns the region. It works the same for both styles.

`"bucket.localhost:4566".indexOf('.')` → 6 (the dot between bucket and localhost)
